The editor will search the given number of folder levels upwards for .kateconfig file and load the settings line from it.
The editor will load given number of blocks (of around 2048 lines) of text into memory; if the filesize is bigger than this the other blocks are swapped  to disk and loaded transparently as-needed.<br> This can cause little delays while navigating in the document; a larger block count increases the editing speed at the cost of memory. <br>For normal usage, just choose the highest possible block count: limit it only if you have problems with the memory usage.

<p>Enables the start of dynamically wrapped lines to be aligned vertically to the indentation level of the first line.  This can help to make code and markup more readable.</p><p>Additionally, this allows you to set a maximum width of the screen, as a percentage, after which dynamically wrapped lines will no longer be vertically aligned.  For example, at 50%, lines whose indentation levels are deeper than 50% of the width of the screen will not have vertical alignment applied to subsequent wrapped lines.</p>
